All Flag Emojis

See Also:FamiliesHolding HandsKissingIn LoveHandshakes

There are many emojis designated to represent flags of countries, regions, and more. This page aims to list all of them, including regional indicator sequences, tag sequences, and pride flags.

Country Flags

 Country flag emojis are made with two regional indicator characters, which represent two-letter country codes defined in ISO 3166-1 alpha-2. They are also called emoji flag sequences or regional indicator sequences.

Regional indicators: 🇦 🇧 🇨 🇩 🇪 🇫 🇬 🇭 🇮 🇯 🇰 🇱 🇲 🇳 🇴 🇵 🇶 🇷 🇸 🇹 🇺 🇻 🇼 🇽 🇾 🇿

Alone, the regional indicator will display as its letter. Invalid combinations will display as either the two letters or a black flag emoji. Below are all valid combinations.

Original 10 Unicode Flags: 🇨🇳 🇩🇪 🇪🇸 🇫🇷 🇬🇧 🇮🇹 🇯🇵 🇰🇷 🇷🇺 🇺🇸

Some flag emojis look the same, such as United States 🇺🇸 and U.S. Outlying Islands 🇺🇲, but they are still considered different characters. These duplicates are often for territories and may be excluded from a device's keyboard to avoid confusion.

Most flags should appear rectangular, with the exception of Nepal 🇳🇵, Switzerland 🇨🇭, and Vatican City 🇻🇦.

Subdivision Flags

 For subdivisions of countries, like states or provinces, a tag sequence can be used, which consists of a Black Flag 🏴 followed by tag characters. The invisible tag characters are a country's two-letter country code, the subdivison code defined in ISO 3166-2, and a Cancel tag.

These flags are not supported anywhere, with a few exceptions:
England 🏴󠁧󠁢󠁥󠁮󠁧󠁿, Scotland 🏴󠁧󠁢󠁳󠁣󠁴󠁿, and Wales 🏴󠁧󠁢󠁷󠁬󠁳󠁿 are supported on all platforms.
Texas 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁴󠁸󠁿 is supported on WhatsApp.
The non-standard ZWJ sequence for Refugee Nation 🏳️‍🟧‍⬛️‍🟧 is also supported on WhatsApp.

For some time, WhatsApp and Instagram used these temporary regional indicator combinations when there were no emoji flags for England 🇽🇪, Scotland 🇽🇸, and Wales 🇽🇼.

Some tag sequences represent regions that already have a flag emoji, such as Puerto Rico (US-PR) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁰󠁲󠁿 🇵🇷.

England (GB-ENG) 🏴󠁧󠁢󠁥󠁮󠁧󠁿 Scotland (GB-SCT) 🏴󠁧󠁢󠁳󠁣󠁴󠁿 Wales (GB-WLS) 🏴󠁧󠁢󠁷󠁬󠁳󠁿 Northern Ireland (GB-NIR) 🏴󠁧󠁢󠁮󠁩󠁲󠁿 Texas (US-TX) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁴󠁸󠁿 Alaska (US-AK) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁡󠁫󠁿 Alabama (US-AL) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁡󠁬󠁿 Arkansas (US-AR) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁡󠁲󠁿 American Samoa (US-AS) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁡󠁳󠁿 Arizona (US-AZ) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁡󠁺󠁿 California (US-CA) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁣󠁡󠁿 Colorado (US-CO) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁣󠁯󠁿 Connecticut (US-CT) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁣󠁴󠁿 Washington DC (US-DC) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁤󠁣󠁿 Delaware (US-DE) 🏴󠁵󠁳󠁤󠁥󠁿 Florida (US-FL) Non-Regional Flags

 Other flags are represented in Unicode. Some have their own designated characters, while others use ZWJ sequences, with zero-width joiners (U+200D) between two or more characters.

Flag characters:
White Flag: 🏳️
Black Flag: 🏴
Chequered Flag / Checkered Flag: 🏁
Triangular Red Flag: 🚩
Golf Flag: ⛳️
ZWJ sequences:
Jolly Roger / Pirate Flag: 🏴‍☠️ (🏴 + ☠️)
Rainbow Flag: 🏳️‍🌈 (🏳️ + 🌈)
Transgender Flag: 🏳️‍⚧️ (🏳️ + ⚧️)

Unicode has said that they will not accept proposals for any new flag emojis, including subdivison and pride flags. New flag emojis can still be added if the United Nations recognizes a country and it is assigned a two-letter country code.
